Arguing as in the proof of Proposition [3.6](#S3.ThmTheorem6 "Proposition 3.6. ‚Ä£ 3.1.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"), we show that ūĚĒľ‚Ąô~‚Äč[supt‚ąą[0,T]|őďt|p]<‚ąě\mathbb{E}^{\tilde{\mathbb{P}}}\Big[\sup\_{t\in[0,T]}|\Gamma\_{t}|^{p}\Big]<\infty
for some p>1p>1.
As for őõ\Lambda, it is clear that it belongs to LūĚĒĹ2‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚd)L^{2}\_{\mathbb{F}}([0,T],\mathbb{R}^{d}) for Ōā\varsigma and Ōą\psi are bounded and ūĚĒľ‚Äč[‚ąę0T‚ąĎi=1dVsi‚Äčd‚Äčs]<‚ąě\mathbb{E}\Big[\int\_{0}^{T}\sum\_{i=1}^{d}V^{i}\_{s}ds\Big]<\infty thanks to ([2.17](#S2.E17 "In Theorem 2.7. ‚Ä£ 2.2 Formulation of the stochastic Market model ‚Ä£ 2 Preliminaries: Multivariate fake stationary affine Volterra models ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")). ‚Ė°\Box

Proof of Theorem [3.5](#S3.ThmTheorem5 "Theorem 3.5. ‚Ä£ 3.1.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"):
We show that JtőĪJ\_{t}^{\alpha} fulfills the martingale optimality principle in Definition [3.2](#S3.ThmTheorem2 "Definition 3.2 (Martingale optimality principle). ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models").
For the first condition, note that őďT=1\Gamma\_{T}=1 and hence JTőĪ=1ő≥‚Äč(XTőĪ)ő≥J\_{T}^{\alpha}=\frac{1}{\gamma}(X\_{T}^{\alpha})^{\gamma}. Since őď0\Gamma\_{0} is a constant independent of őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in{\mathcal{A}}, J0őĪ=x0ő≥ő≥‚Äčőď0J^{\alpha}\_{0}=\frac{x^{\gamma}\_{0}}{\gamma}\Gamma\_{0} is a constant independent of őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in{\mathcal{A}} and consequently, the second condition is also satisfied.
In order to show that the third condition is fulfilled, we apply It√ī‚Äôs formula on JtőĪJ\_{t}^{\alpha}. We have:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | d‚ÄčJtőĪ=(XtőĪ)ő≥ő≥‚Äčőďt‚Äč[(‚ąíő≥‚Äčr‚Äč(t)‚ąíő≥2‚Äč(1‚ąíő≥)‚Äč(|őĽt|2+őī2‚Äč|ő£‚Äčőõt|2))‚Äčd‚Äčt+őī‚Äčőõt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčW~t]\displaystyle dJ\_{t}^{\alpha}=\;\frac{(X\_{t}^{\alpha})^{\gamma}}{\gamma}\Gamma\_{t}\Big[\big(-\gamma r(t)-\frac{\gamma}{2(1-\gamma)}(\left|\lambda\_{t}\right|^{2}+\delta^{2}\left|\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right|^{2})\big)dt+\delta\Lambda\_{t}^{\top}d\widetilde{W}\_{t}\Big] |  |
|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | +(XtőĪ)ő≥‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčőďt‚Äč(ő≥‚ÄčXtőĪ‚Äč(r‚Äč(t)+őĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĽt)+ő≥‚Äč(ő≥‚ąí1)2‚ÄčXtőĪ‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĪt)‚Äčd‚Äčt+őďt‚Äč(XtőĪ)ő≥‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčBt+őī‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äč(ő£‚Äčőõt)‚Äč(XtőĪ)ő≥‚Äčőďt‚Äčd‚Äčt\displaystyle\hskip 14.22636pt+\frac{(X\_{t}^{\alpha})^{\gamma-1}}{\gamma}\Gamma\_{t}\Big(\gamma X\_{t}^{\alpha}\big(r(t)+\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\lambda\_{t}\big)+\frac{\gamma(\gamma-1)}{2}X\_{t}^{\alpha}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\alpha\_{t}\Big)dt+\Gamma\_{t}(X\_{t}^{\alpha})^{\gamma}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}dB\_{t}+\delta\alpha^{\top}\_{t}\left(\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right)(X\_{t}^{\alpha})^{\gamma}\Gamma\_{t}dt |  |
|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | =JtőĪ‚Äč(ő≥‚Äč(ő≥‚ąí1)2‚ÄčőĪ‚ä§‚ÄčőĪ+ő≥‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĽt+őī‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äč(ő£‚Äčőõt)‚ąíő≥2‚Äč(1‚ąíő≥)‚Äč(|őĽt|2+őī2‚Äč|ő£‚Äčőõt|2)‚ąíőī‚Äčő≥(1‚ąíő≥)‚Äčőõt‚ä§‚Äčő£‚ÄčőĽt)‚Äčd‚Äčt\displaystyle\hskip 28.45274pt=\;J\_{t}^{\alpha}\Big(\frac{\gamma(\gamma-1)}{2}\alpha^{\top}\alpha+\gamma\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\lambda\_{t}+\delta\alpha^{\top}\_{t}\left(\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right)-\frac{\gamma}{2(1-\gamma)}(\left|\lambda\_{t}\right|^{2}+\delta^{2}\left|\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right|^{2})-\delta\frac{\gamma}{(1-\gamma)}\Lambda\_{t}^{\top}\Sigma\lambda\_{t}\Big)dt |  |
|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | +ő≥‚ÄčJtőĪ‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčBt+JtőĪ‚Äčőī‚Äčőõt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčWt=JtőĪ‚ÄčDt‚Äč(őĪt)‚Äčd‚Äčt+ő≥‚ÄčJtőĪ‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčBt+JtőĪ‚Äčőī‚Äčőõt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčWt.\displaystyle\hskip 28.45274pt+\gamma J\_{t}^{\alpha}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}dB\_{t}+J\_{t}^{\alpha}\delta\Lambda\_{t}^{\top}dW\_{t}=J\_{t}^{\alpha}D\_{t}(\alpha\_{t})dt+\gamma J\_{t}^{\alpha}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}dB\_{t}+J\_{t}^{\alpha}\delta\Lambda\_{t}^{\top}dW\_{t}. |  |

where the drift factor takes the form:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Dt‚Äč(őĪ)=\displaystyle D\_{t}(\alpha)= | ő≥‚Äč(ő≥‚ąí1)2‚ÄčőĪ‚ä§‚ÄčőĪ+ő≥‚ÄčőĪ‚ä§‚Äč(őĽt+őī‚Äčő£‚Äčőõt)‚ąíő≥2‚Äč(1‚ąíő≥)‚Äč|őĽt+őī‚Äčő£‚Äčőõt|2.\displaystyle\frac{\gamma(\gamma-1)}{2}\alpha^{\top}\alpha+\gamma\alpha^{\top}\big(\lambda\_{t}+\delta\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\big)-\frac{\gamma}{2(1-\gamma)}\left|\lambda\_{t}+\delta\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right|^{2}. |  |

Differentiating Dt‚Äč(őĪ)D\_{t}(\alpha) with respect to őĪ\alpha and checking the second order condition, one obtains the maximizer őĪt‚ąó=11‚ąíő≥‚Äč(őĽt+őī‚Äčő£‚Äčőõt)\alpha^{\*}\_{t}=\frac{1}{1-\gamma}\left(\lambda\_{t}+\delta\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right) for every t‚ąą[0,T]t\in[0,T] that is the strategy given by Equation ([3.39](#S3.E39 "In Theorem 3.5. ‚Ä£ 3.1.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")).

Evaluating the drift factor DtD\_{t} at őĪt‚ąó\alpha^{\*}\_{t} show that Dt‚Äč(őĪt‚ąó)D\_{t}(\alpha^{\*}\_{t}) vanishes to 0. Note Dt‚Äč(őĪ)D\_{t}(\alpha) is a quadratic function on őĪ\alpha and ő≥‚ąí1<0\gamma-1<0. As Dt‚Äč(őĪt‚ąó)=0D\_{t}(\alpha^{\*}\_{t})=0, then Dt‚Äč(őĪt)‚Č§0D\_{t}(\alpha\_{t})\leq 0 for any admissible strategy őĪ\alpha.
Moreover, solving the stochastic differential equation for JtőĪJ\_{t}^{\alpha} yields

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ‚ąÄt‚ąą[0,T]JtőĪ=őď0‚Äčx0ő≥ő≥‚Äče‚ąę0tDs‚Äč(őĪs)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčFtőĪwhere\displaystyle\hskip 142.26378pt\forall\,t\in[0,T]\quad J\_{t}^{\alpha}=\frac{\Gamma\_{0}x\_{0}^{\gamma}}{\gamma}e^{\int\_{0}^{t}D\_{s}(\alpha\_{s})\,ds}F\_{t}^{\alpha}\quad\text{where} |  | (5.88) |
|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | FtőĪ=‚Ąį‚Äč(‚ąę0tő≥‚ÄčőĪs‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs+őī‚Äčőõs‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčWs)=exp‚Ā°(‚ąí12‚Äč‚ąę0t(ő≥2‚Äč|őĪs|2+őī2‚Äč|őõs|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+ő≥‚Äč‚ąę0tőĪs‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs+őī‚Äč‚ąę0tőõs‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎWs).\displaystyle F\_{t}^{\alpha}=\mathcal{E}\big(\int\_{0}^{t}\gamma\,\alpha\_{s}^{\top}\,dB\_{s}+\delta\,\Lambda\_{s}^{\top}\,dW\_{s}\big)=\operatorname{exp}\Big(-\frac{1}{2}\int^{t}\_{0}\big(\gamma^{2}\left|\alpha\_{s}\right|^{2}+\delta^{2}\left|\Lambda\_{s}\right|^{2}\big)ds+\gamma\int\_{0}^{t}\alpha\_{s}^{\top}dB\_{s}+\delta\int\_{0}^{t}\Lambda\_{s}^{\top}dW\_{s}\Big). |  |

Now, since Ds‚Äč(őĪs)‚Č§0D\_{s}(\alpha\_{s})\leq 0, e‚ąę0tDs‚Äč(őĪs)‚ÄčūĚĎĎse^{\int^{t}\_{0}D\_{s}(\alpha\_{s})ds} is a non-increasing function. By our assumptions on the admissible strategies [3.3](#S3.ThmTheorem3 "Definition 3.3. ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") and Proposition [3.4](#S3.ThmTheorem4 "Proposition 3.4. ‚Ä£ 3.1.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"),
(őĪ,őõ)‚ąąLūĚĒĹ2,l‚Äčo‚Äčc‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚd)\left(\alpha,\Lambda\right)\in{L^{2,loc}\_{\mathbb{F}}([0,T],\mathbb{R}^{d})} and thus the stochastic exponential FtőĪF\_{t}^{\alpha} is a local martingale (which follows from the basic properties of the Dool√©ans-Dade exponential). Therefore, there exists a sequence of stopping times {ŌĄn}n‚Č•1\{\tau\_{n}\}\_{n\geq 1} satisfying limn‚Üí‚ąěŌĄn=T\lim\_{n\rightarrow\infty}\tau\_{n}=T, ‚Ąô\mathbb{P}-a.s., such that

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[Jt‚ąßŌĄnőĪ|‚ĄĪs]‚Č§Js‚ąßŌĄnőĪ,s‚Č§t‚Č§T,\mathbb{E}[J^{\alpha}\_{t\wedge\tau\_{n}}|{\mathcal{F}}\_{s}]\leq J^{\alpha}\_{s\wedge\tau\_{n}},\quad s\leq t\leq T, |  |

for every nn. Moreover, since JtőĪJ^{\alpha}\_{t} is bounded from below by 0 ( JtőĪ‚Č•0J\_{t}^{\alpha}\geq 0), applying Fatou‚Äôs Lemma for n‚Üí‚ąěn\rightarrow\infty, we deduce that JtőĪJ^{\alpha}\_{t} is a supermartingale for every arbitrary admissible strategy őĪ\alpha.
It remains to show that JtőĪ‚ąóJ\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}} is a true martingale for the optimal strategy őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*} in which case e‚ąę0tDs‚Äč(őĪs‚ąó)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs=1e^{\int\_{0}^{t}D\_{s}(\alpha\_{s}^{\*})ds}=1 and hence JtőĪ‚ąó=őď0‚Äčx0ő≥ő≥‚ÄčFtőĪ‚ąóJ\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}}=\frac{\Gamma\_{0}x\_{0}^{\gamma}}{\gamma}F\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}}.

For őĪt=őĪt‚ąó\alpha\_{t}=\alpha^{\*}\_{t}, FtőĪ‚ąóF\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}} is a martingale by Lemma [5.1](#S5.ThmTheorem1 "Lemma 5.1 (Martingale property of stochastic exponentials). ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") with g1,i‚Äč(t)=ő≥1‚ąíő≥‚ÄčŌĀi‚Äčőłi+(1+ő≥1‚ąíő≥‚ÄčŌĀi2)‚ÄčőĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(t)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąít)‚ąąL‚ąě‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚ)g\_{1,i}(t)=\frac{\gamma}{1-\gamma}\rho\_{i}\theta\_{i}+(1+\frac{\gamma}{1-\gamma}\rho\_{i}^{2})\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(t)\psi^{i}(T-t)\in L^{\infty}([0,T],\mathbb{R}) and g2,i‚Äč(t)=ő≥1‚ąíő≥‚Äč1‚ąíŌĀi2‚Äč(őłi+ŌĀi‚ÄčőĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(t)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąít))‚ąąL‚ąě‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚ)g\_{2,i}(t)=\frac{\gamma}{1-\gamma}\sqrt{1-\rho\_{i}^{2}}\big(\theta\_{i}+\rho\_{i}\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(t)\psi^{i}(T-t)\big)\in L^{\infty}([0,T],\mathbb{R}) for 1‚Č§i‚Č§d1\leq i\leq d.
Subsequently, JtőĪ‚ąóJ^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{t} is a true martingale. We have verified all conditions required by martingale optimality principle, except for the admissibility of őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*}, which follows directly from Step 1 in the proof of Theorem [3.7](#S3.ThmTheorem7 "Theorem 3.7. ‚Ä£ 3.1.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") in the more general setting, as the arguments are similar. The proof is complete. ‚Ė°\Box

Proof of Theorem [3.7](#S3.ThmTheorem7 "Theorem 3.7. ‚Ä£ 3.1.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"):

Step 1 (Proof of Admissibility:)
We begin by proving the admissibility of the candidate in equation ([3.49](#S3.E49 "In 3.1.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) for the optimal portfolio strategy őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*}, and, en route, we deduce the bound in equation ([3.52](#S3.E52 "In Theorem 3.7. ‚Ä£ 3.1.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")).

In order to show that őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*} is admissible, we have to show that (a), (b), (c) of Definition [3.3](#S3.ThmTheorem3 "Definition 3.3. ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") hold. Part (a) is true because ([3.30](#S3.E30 "In 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) has a unique solution ([3.31](#S3.E31 "In 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) in terms of (S,V,B)(S,V,B).
For part (b) it suffices to show that ūĚĒľ‚Äč[supt‚ąą[0,T]‚Ā°|XtőĪ‚ąó|p]<‚ąě\mathbb{E}[\operatorname{sup}\_{t\in[0,T]}|X\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}}|^{p}]<\infty for every p>0p>0.
Inserting the explicit solution of the control problem into ([3.30](#S3.E30 "In 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"))
and using It√ī‚Äôs lemma (or equivalently into ([3.31](#S3.E31 "In 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"))), the unique continuous solution of the controlled wealth process XőĪ‚ąóX^{\alpha^{\*}} is given by :

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | XtőĪ‚ąó=x0‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąę0t(r‚Äč(s)+őĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčőĽs‚ąí12‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąę0tőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs).X\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}}=x\_{0}\exp\!\left(\int\_{0}^{t}\Big(r(s)+\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\lambda\_{s}-\tfrac{1}{2}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}\Big)\,ds+\int\_{0}^{t}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\,dB\_{s}\right). |  | (5.89) |

Observe by virtue of ([3.27](#S3.E27 "In 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")), that the Dol√©ans-Dade exponential ‚Ąį‚Äč(‚ąę0‚čÖőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs)\mathcal{E}\left(\int\_{0}^{\cdot}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}dB\_{s}\right) satisfies Novikov‚Äôs condition, and is therefore a true martingale (see also Lemma [5.2](#S5.ThmTheorem2 "Lemma 5.2 (Martingale property). ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")).
By virtue of the Cauchy-Schwarz inequality, and then Doob‚Äôs maximal inequality in the second line, for every p>1p>1

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[supt‚ąą[0,T]|XtőĪ‚ąó|p]‚Č§x0p‚ÄčūĚĒľ‚Äč[supt‚ąą[0,T]|e‚ąę0t(r‚Äč(s)+őĽs‚ä§‚ÄčőĪs‚ąó)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs|2‚Äčp]12‚ÄčūĚĒľ‚Äč[supt‚ąą[0,T]|exp‚Ā°(‚ąí12‚Äč‚ąę0t|őĪs‚ąó|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąę0tőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs)|2‚Äčp]12\displaystyle\,\mathbb{E}\Big[\sup\_{t\in[0,T]}|X^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{t}|^{p}\Big]\leq x\_{0}^{p}\mathbb{E}\Big[\sup\_{t\in[0,T]}\big|e^{\int\_{0}^{t}{\left(r(s)+\lambda\_{s}^{\top}\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right)}ds}\big|^{2p}\Big]^{\frac{1}{2}}\mathbb{E}\Big[\sup\_{t\in[0,T]}\Big|\exp\Big(-\tfrac{1}{2}\int^{t}\_{0}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}ds+\int^{t}\_{0}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\,dB\_{s}\Big)\Big|^{2p}\Big]^{\frac{1}{2}} |  |
|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ‚Č§x0p‚Äčep‚Äč‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äč(2‚Äčp2‚Äčp‚ąí1)p‚ÄčūĚĒľ‚Äč[e2‚Äčp‚Äč‚ąę0T|őĽs‚ä§‚ÄčőĪs‚ąó|‚ÄčūĚĎĎs]12‚ÄčūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąíp‚Äč‚ąę0T|őĪs‚ąó|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+2‚Äčp‚Äč‚ąę0TőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs)]12.\displaystyle\hskip 65.44142pt\leq x\_{0}^{p}e^{p\int\_{0}^{T}r(s)ds}\Big(\frac{2p}{2p-1}\Big)^{p}\mathbb{E}\Big[e^{2p\int\_{0}^{T}|\lambda\_{s}^{\top}\alpha\_{s}^{\*}|ds}\Big]^{\frac{1}{2}}\mathbb{E}\Big[\exp\Big(-p\int^{T}\_{0}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}ds+2p\int^{T}\_{0}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\,dB\_{s}\Big)\Big]^{\frac{1}{2}}. |  |

The first term is finite on the first hand by condition ([3.27](#S3.E27 "In 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) with constant a‚Äč(p1‚ąíő≥)=p1‚ąíő≥‚Äč(2+|ő£|)a(\frac{p}{1-\gamma})=\frac{p}{1-\gamma}\left(2+|\Sigma|\right) and owing to the elementary arithmetic mean-geometric mean (AM-GM) inequality |a‚Äčb|‚Č§(|a|2+|b|2)/2|ab|\leq(|a|^{2}+|b|^{2})/2

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[e2‚Äčp‚Äč‚ąę0T|őĽs‚ä§‚ÄčőĪs‚ąó|‚ÄčūĚĎĎs]‚Č§ūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(a‚Äč(p1‚ąíő≥)‚Äč‚ąę0T(|őĽs|2+|őõs|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)]<‚ąě,\mathbb{E}\Big[e^{2p\int\_{0}^{T}|\lambda\_{s}^{\top}\alpha\_{s}^{\*}|ds}\Big]\leq\mathbb{E}\left[\exp\left({a(\frac{p}{1-\gamma})\int\_{0}^{T}\left(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}\right)ds}\right)\right]<\infty, |  | (5.90) |

and, on the other hand, the second term is also finite since by virtue of H√∂lder‚Äôs inequality,

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[e‚ąí‚ąę0Tp‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąę0T2‚Äčp‚ÄčőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs]\displaystyle\mathbb{E}\Big[e^{-\int^{T}\_{0}p\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}ds+\int^{T}\_{0}2p\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\,dB\_{s}}\Big] | ‚Č§(ūĚĒľ‚Äč[e(8‚Äčp2‚ąí2‚Äčp)‚Äč‚ąę0T|őĪs‚ąó|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs])1/2‚Äč(ūĚĒľ‚Äč[e‚ąí8‚Äčp2‚Äč‚ąę0T|őĪs‚ąó|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+4‚Äčp‚Äč‚ąę0TőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs])1/2\displaystyle\leq\left(\mathbb{E}\Big[e^{(8p^{2}-2p)\int^{T}\_{0}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}ds}\Big]\right)^{1/2}\left(\mathbb{E}\Big[e^{-8p^{2}\int^{T}\_{0}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}ds+4p\int^{T}\_{0}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\,dB\_{s}}\Big]\right)^{1/2} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | ‚Č§(ūĚĒľ‚Äč[ea‚Äč(p1‚ąíő≥)‚Äč‚ąę0T(|őĽs|2+|őõs|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs])1/2√ó1<‚ąě.\displaystyle\leq\left(\mathbb{E}\left[e^{a(\frac{p}{1-\gamma})\int\_{0}^{T}\left(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}\right)ds}\right]\right)^{1/2}\times 1<\infty. |  |

with constant a‚Äč(p1‚ąíő≥)=2‚Äč(8‚Äč(11‚ąíő≥)2‚ąí2‚Äčp1‚ąíő≥)‚Äč(1+|ő£|2)a(\frac{p}{1-\gamma})=2(8\big(\frac{1}{1-\gamma}\big)^{2}{-2\frac{p}{1-\gamma}})\left(1+|{\Sigma}|^{2}\right) and where we used Jensen‚Äôs inequality to bound

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | |őĪs‚ąó|2=(11‚ąíő≥)2‚Äč|őĽs+ő£‚Äčőõs|2‚Č§2‚Äč(11‚ąíő≥)2‚Äč(|őĽs|2+|ő£‚Äčőõs|2)‚Č§2‚Äč(11‚ąíő≥)2‚Äč(1+|ő£|2)‚Äč(|őĽs|2+|őõs|2).\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}=\big(\frac{1}{1-\gamma}\big)^{2}|\lambda\_{s}+\Sigma\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}\leq 2\big(\frac{1}{1-\gamma}\big)^{2}(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Sigma\Lambda\_{s}|^{2})\leq 2\big(\frac{1}{1-\gamma}\big)^{2}(1+|\Sigma|^{2})(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}). |  | (5.91) |

then noticing that (11‚ąíő≥)2‚Äč(8‚Äčp2‚ąí2‚Äčp)‚Č§8‚Äč(p1‚ąíő≥)2‚ąí2‚Äčp1‚ąíő≥\big(\frac{1}{1-\gamma}\big)^{2}(8p^{2}{-2p})\leq 8\big(\frac{p}{1-\gamma}\big)^{2}{-2\frac{p}{1-\gamma}} for all p>1,ő≥‚ąą(0,1)p>1,\,\gamma\in(0,1), together with condition ([3.27](#S3.E27 "In 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) and Novikov‚Äôs condition to the Dol√©ans-Dade exponential ‚Ąį‚Äč(4‚Äčp‚Äč‚ąę0‚čÖőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs)\mathcal{E}(4p\int\_{0}^{{\cdot}}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}dB\_{s}).
This leads to Part (c).
ūĚĒľ‚Äč[supt‚ąą[0,T]|XtőĪ‚ąó|p]<‚ąě\mathbb{E}\Big[\sup\_{t\in[0,T]}|X^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{t}|^{p}\Big]<\infty is proved. It becomes straightforward to verify őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*} is admissible. We are left to prove that őĪ‚ąó‚ąąLūĚĒĹ2‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚd)\alpha^{\*}\in L^{2}\_{\mathbb{F}}([0,T],\mathbb{R}^{d}). We have

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[‚ąę0T|őĪs‚ąó|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs]\displaystyle\mathbb{E}\left[\int\_{0}^{T}|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}|^{2}ds\right] | =ūĚĒľ‚Äč[‚ąę0T(11‚ąíő≥)2‚Äč|őĽs+ő£‚Äčőõs|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs]‚Č§ūĚĒľ‚Äč[2‚Äč(11‚ąíő≥)2‚Äč(1+|ő£|2)‚Äč‚ąę0T(|őĽs|2+|őõs|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs]<‚ąě,\displaystyle{=}\mathbb{E}\left[\int\_{0}^{T}\big(\frac{1}{1-\gamma}\big)^{2}|\lambda\_{s}+\Sigma\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}ds\right]\leq\mathbb{E}\left[2\big(\frac{1}{1-\gamma}\big)^{2}(1+|\Sigma|^{2})\int\_{0}^{T}\left(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}\right)ds\right]<\infty, |  |

where the last term is finite due to condition ([3.27](#S3.E27 "In 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) and the inequality |z|q‚Č§cq‚Äče|z|,‚ąÄq‚Č•1|z|^{q}\leq c\_{q}e^{|z|},\;\forall\,q\geq 1.

Step 2 (Proof of the equality (1):)
Let‚Äôs us consider the Problem ([3.33](#S3.E33 "In 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) with an arbitrary strategy őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in\mathcal{A} from Definition [3.3](#S3.ThmTheorem3 "Definition 3.3. ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models").

where the drift factor takes the form Dt‚Äč(őĪt)=ő≥‚Äč(ő≥‚ąí1)2‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĪt+ő≥‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äčht‚ąíő≥2‚Äč(1‚ąíő≥)‚Äčht‚ä§‚Äčht.D\_{t}(\alpha\_{t})=\frac{\gamma(\gamma-1)}{2}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\alpha\_{t}+\gamma\alpha\_{t}^{\top}h\_{t}-\frac{\gamma}{2(1-\gamma)}h\_{t}^{\top}h\_{t}.

Step 3 (Proof of the inequality (2):)
Recall that the SDE for the wealth process ([3.30](#S3.E30 "In 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) can be solved explicitly so as to admit the representation

where we write the arbitrary admissible strategy (őĪt)t‚ąą[0,T](\alpha\_{t})\_{t\in[0,T]} in terms of the optimal strategy őĪt‚ąó=11‚ąíő≥‚Äč(őĽt+ő£‚Äčőõt)\alpha^{\*}\_{t}=\frac{1}{1-\gamma}\left(\lambda\_{t}+\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right) for every t‚ąą[0,T]t\in[0,T] and some remainder (őĪ^t)t‚ąą[0,T](\hat{\alpha}\_{t})\_{t\in[0,T]} i.e. őĪt=őĪt‚ąó+őĪ^t\alpha\_{t}=\alpha\_{t}^{\*}+\hat{\alpha}\_{t} for every t‚ąą[0,T]t\in[0,T].

Under the probability measure ‚Ąö\mathbb{Q} defined in ([5.105](#S5.E105 "In 5.2 Proofs of Proposition 3.9 and Theorems 3.10 and 3.12 ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")), the processes B^t:=Bt‚ąíő≥‚Äč‚ąę0tőĪs‚ÄčūĚĎĎs\widehat{B}\_{t}:=B\_{t}-\gamma\int\_{0}^{t}\alpha\_{s}ds and

|  |  |  |

|  | W^t:=ő£‚ÄčB^t+I‚ąíő£‚ä§‚Äčő£‚ÄčBt‚üā=Wt‚ąíő≥‚Äč‚ąę0tő£‚ÄčőĪs‚ÄčūĚĎĎs=Wt‚ąíő≥‚Äč‚ąę0tő£‚ÄčőĪs‚ąó‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ąíő≥‚Äč‚ąę0tő£‚ÄčőĪ^s‚ÄčūĚĎĎs,\widehat{W}\_{t}:=\Sigma\widehat{B}\_{t}+\sqrt{I-\Sigma^{\top}\Sigma}B^{\perp}\_{t}=W\_{t}-\gamma\int\_{0}^{t}\Sigma\alpha\_{s}ds=W\_{t}-\gamma\int\_{0}^{t}\Sigma\alpha^{\*}\_{s}ds-\gamma\int\_{0}^{t}\Sigma\hat{\alpha}\_{s}ds, |  |

are standard Wiener processes thanks to the Cameron‚ÄďMartin‚ÄďGirsanov and Girsanov theorem respectively theorem.
The dynamics of the variance process VV under ‚Ąö\mathbb{Q} can thus be written as

one gets using Equation ([3.44](#S3.E44 "In Proposition 3.6. ‚Ä£ 3.1.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.1 Optimal strategy for the power utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"))

Remark: (Alternative Proof of the equality (1):) At this stage, note that if the admissible strategy őĪ\alpha is optimal, i.e. őĪ=őĪ‚ąó\alpha=\alpha^{\*} so that ŌÄ^‚Č°0\hat{\pi}\equiv 0 and ‚Ąö‚Č°‚Ąö‚ąó\mathbb{Q}\equiv\mathbb{Q}^{\*} in ([5.94](#S5.E94 "In 5.1 Proofs of Proposition 3.4 and Theorems 3.5 and 3.7 ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")), then Equation ([5.96](#S5.E96 "In 5.1 Proofs of Proposition 3.4 and Theorems 3.5 and 3.7 ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) becomes:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | x0‚ąíő≥‚ÄčūĚĒľx0,V0‚Äč[(XTőĪ‚ąó)ő≥]=exp‚Ā°(ő≥‚Äč‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0T(ő≥‚Äčőłi22‚Äč(1‚ąíő≥)+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg0i‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)\displaystyle x\_{0}^{-\gamma}\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}[{(X\_{T}^{\alpha^{\*}})^{\gamma}}]=\exp\Big(\gamma\int\_{0}^{T}r(s)ds+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\big(\frac{\gamma\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2(1-\gamma)}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)g^{i}\_{0}(s)ds\Big) |  |

Since Ōą\psi is continuous, it is bounded and therefore the stochastic exponential is a true ‚Ąö‚ąó\mathbb{Q}^{\*}- martingale with expectation 11 by Lemma [5.1](#S5.ThmTheorem1 "Lemma 5.1 (Martingale property of stochastic exponentials). ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") with g2=0g\_{2}=0 and g1,i‚Äč(s)=őĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąís)‚ąąL‚ąě‚Äč(‚ĄĚ+,‚ĄĚ)g\_{1,i}(s)=\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s)\in L^{\infty}(\mathbb{R}^{+},\mathbb{R}) . Thus we get

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľx0,V0‚Äč[1ő≥‚Äč(XTőĪ‚ąó)ő≥]=x0ő≥ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(ő≥‚Äč‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0T(ő≥‚Äčőłi22‚Äč(1‚ąíő≥)+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg0i‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs).\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}\Big[{\frac{1}{\gamma}(X\_{T}^{\alpha^{\*}})^{\gamma}}\Big]=\frac{x\_{0}^{\gamma}}{\gamma}\exp\Big(\gamma\int\_{0}^{T}r(s)ds+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\big(\frac{\gamma\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2(1-\gamma)}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)g^{i}\_{0}(s)ds\Big). |  |

This again completes the first part of the proof (equality (1)).

Coming back to the proof of the inequality (2) for arbitrary admissible portfolio strategies őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in\mathcal{A}, from Equation ([5.96](#S5.E96 "In 5.1 Proofs of Proposition 3.4 and Theorems 3.5 and 3.7 ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")), since VsV\_{s} is positive
definite and ő≥‚ąą(0,1)\gamma\in(0,1), the term ‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0Tő≥‚Äč(ő≥‚ąí1)2‚ÄčŌÄ^s,i2‚ÄčVsi‚ÄčūĚĎĎs=‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0Tő≥‚Äč(ő≥‚ąí1)2‚ÄčőĪ^s,i2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{\gamma(\gamma-1)}{2}\hat{\pi}\_{s,i}^{2}V^{i}\_{s}\,ds=\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{\gamma(\gamma-1)}{2}\hat{\alpha}\_{s,i}^{2}\,ds has to be less than or equal to 0 so that

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | x0‚ąíő≥‚ÄčūĚĒľx0,V0‚Äč[(XTőĪ)ő≥]‚Č§exp‚Ā°(ő≥‚Äč‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0T(ő≥‚Äčőłi22‚Äč(1‚ąíő≥)+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg0i‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)\displaystyle x\_{0}^{-\gamma}\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}[{(X\_{T}^{\alpha})^{\gamma}}]\leq\exp\Big(\gamma\int\_{0}^{T}r(s)ds+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\big(\frac{\gamma\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2(1-\gamma)}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)g^{i}\_{0}(s)ds\Big) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | √óūĚĒľx0,V0‚Ąö‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąí‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0TőĹi22‚Äč(Ōāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąís))2‚ÄčVsi‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0TőĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąís)‚ÄčVsi‚ÄčūĚĎĎW^si)].\displaystyle\hskip 62.59596pt\times\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}^{\mathbb{Q}}\Big[\exp\Big(-\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{\nu\_{i}^{2}}{2}(\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s))^{2}V\_{s}^{i}ds+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s)\sqrt{V\_{s}^{i}}d\widehat{W}^{i}\_{s}\Big)\Big]. |  |

Since the stochastic exponential
is a ‚Ąö\mathbb{Q}-martingale with expectation 11 still by Lemma [5.1](#S5.ThmTheorem1 "Lemma 5.1 (Martingale property of stochastic exponentials). ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"), we finally obtain that for every őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in\mathcal{A}

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľx0,V0‚Äč[1ő≥‚Äč(XTőĪ)ő≥]‚Č§x0ő≥ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(ő≥‚Äč‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0T(ő≥‚Äčőłi22‚Äč(1‚ąíő≥)+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg0i‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs).\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}\Big[{\frac{1}{\gamma}(X\_{T}^{\alpha})^{\gamma}}\Big]\leq\frac{x\_{0}^{\gamma}}{\gamma}\exp\Big(\gamma\int\_{0}^{T}r(s)ds+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\big(\frac{\gamma\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2(1-\gamma)}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)g^{i}\_{0}(s)ds\Big). |  |

which completes the proof. ‚Ė°\Box

### 5.2 Proofs of Proposition [3.9](#S3.ThmTheorem9 "Proposition 3.9. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") and Theorems [3.10](#S3.ThmTheorem10 "Theorem 3.10. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") and [3.12](#S3.ThmTheorem12 "Theorem 3.12. ‚Ä£ 3.2.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")

Proof of Proposition [3.9](#S3.ThmTheorem9 "Proposition 3.9. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") : Note that if 1‚ąíŌĀ2=01-\rho^{2}=0, then őďt‚Č§1\Gamma\_{t}\leq 1, ‚Ąô~\tilde{\mathbb{P}}-a.s.. If rather 1‚ąíŌĀ2>01-\rho^{2}>0, we write for every 0‚Č§t‚Č§T0\leq t\leq T:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | őďt1‚ąíŌĀ2=ūĚĒľ‚Ąô~‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąí1‚ąíŌĀ22‚Äč‚ąętT|őĽs|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)|‚ĄĪt]=ūĚĒľ‚Ąô~‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąí1‚ąíŌĀ22‚Äč‚ąętT‚ąĎi=1dőłi2‚ÄčVsi‚Äčd‚Äčs)‚ą£‚ĄĪt],\Gamma\_{t}^{1-\rho^{2}}=\mathbb{E}^{\tilde{\mathbb{P}}}\Big[\operatorname{exp}\Big(-\frac{1-\rho^{2}}{2}\int\_{t}^{T}\left|\lambda\_{s}\right|^{2}ds\Big)|\mathcal{F}\_{t}\Big]=\mathbb{E}^{\tilde{\mathbb{P}}}\Big[\exp\Big(-\frac{1-\rho^{2}}{2}\int\_{t}^{T}\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\theta\_{i}^{2}V^{i}\_{s}ds\Big)\mid\mathcal{F}\_{t}\Big], |  | (5.97) |

which ensures that őďt‚Č§1\Gamma\_{t}\leq 1, ‚Ąô~‚ąía.s.\tilde{\mathbb{P}}-a.s., since V‚ąą‚ĄĚ+dV\in\mathbb{R}^{d}\_{+}. An application of the exponential-affine transform formula in (Gnabeyeu, [2026](#bib.bib14), Theorem A.4) with ‚Ą≥‚ąčm‚Äč(d‚Äčs):=‚ąí1‚ąíŌĀ22‚Äčőł‚äôőł‚ÄčLebd‚Äč(d‚Äčs)\mathcal{M}\ni m(\,\mathrm{d}s):=-\frac{1-\rho^{2}}{2}\theta\odot\theta\,{\rm Leb}\_{d}(\,\mathrm{d}s) (where ‚äô\odot denote the Hadamard (pointwise or component-wise) product) yields:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Ąô~‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąętT‚ąí1‚ąíŌĀ22‚Äč‚ąĎi=1dőłi2‚ÄčVsi‚Äčd‚Äčs)‚ą£‚ĄĪt]=exp‚Ā°(‚ąĎi=1d‚ąętT(‚ąí1‚ąíŌĀ22‚Äčőłi2+F~i‚Äč(s,Ōą~‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg~ti‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)\mathbb{E}^{\tilde{\mathbb{P}}}\Big[\exp\Big(\int\_{t}^{T}-\frac{1-\rho^{2}}{2}\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\theta\_{i}^{2}V^{i}\_{s}ds\Big)\mid\mathcal{F}\_{t}\Big]=\exp\Big(\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{t}^{T}\big(-\frac{1-\rho^{2}}{2}\theta\_{i}^{2}+\tilde{F}\_{i}(s,\tilde{\psi}(T-s))\big)\tilde{g}^{i}\_{t}(s)ds\Big) |  | (5.98) |

where g~=(g~1,‚Ä¶,g~d)‚ä§\tilde{g}=(\tilde{g}^{1},\ldots,\tilde{g}^{d})^{\top}, given as in ([2.19](#S2.E19 "In 2.2 Formulation of the stochastic Market model ‚Ä£ 2 Preliminaries: Multivariate fake stationary affine Volterra models ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"))‚Äď ([2.20](#S2.E20 "In 2.2 Formulation of the stochastic Market model ‚Ä£ 2 Preliminaries: Multivariate fake stationary affine Volterra models ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) denotes the adjusted conditional ‚Ąô~\tilde{\mathbb{P}}-expected variance and

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | F~i‚Äč(s,Ōą~)=‚ąíŌĀ‚Äčőłi‚ÄčőĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌą~i+(D‚ä§‚ÄčŌą~)i+őĹi22‚Äč(Ōāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌą~i)2,i=1,‚Ä¶,d,\tilde{F}\_{i}(s,\tilde{\psi})=-\rho\theta\_{i}\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(s)\tilde{\psi}^{i}+(D^{\top}\tilde{\psi})\_{i}+\frac{\nu\_{i}^{2}}{2}(\varsigma^{i}(s)\tilde{\psi}^{i})^{2},\quad i=1,\ldots,d, |  |

and
Ōą~‚ąąC‚Äč([0,T],(‚ĄĚd)‚ąó)\tilde{\psi}\in C([0,T],(\mathbb{R}^{d})^{\*}) solves the inhomogeneous Ricatti-Volterra equation

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Ōą~i‚Äč(t)\displaystyle\tilde{\psi}^{i}(t) | =‚ąę0tKi‚Äč(t‚ąís)‚Äč(‚ąíőłi2‚Äč(1‚ąíŌĀ2)2+F~i‚Äč(T‚ąís,Ōą~‚Äč(s)))‚ÄčūĚĎĎs,i=1,‚Ä¶,d.\displaystyle=\int\_{0}^{t}K\_{i}(t-s)\big(-\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}(1-\rho^{2})}{2}+\tilde{F}\_{i}(T-s,\tilde{\psi}(s))\big)ds,\quad i=1,\ldots,d. |  | (5.99) |

Setting Ōą~=(1‚ąíŌĀ2)‚ÄčŌą\tilde{\psi}=(1-\rho^{2})\psi implies that F~i‚Äč(s,Ōą~)=(1‚ąíŌĀ2)‚ÄčFi‚Äč(s,Ōą)i=1,‚Ä¶,d\tilde{F}\_{i}(s,\tilde{\psi})=(1-\rho^{2})F\_{i}(s,\psi)\quad i=1,\ldots,d, where FiF\_{i} is given in ([3.58](#S3.E58 "In Proposition 3.9. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")).
Therefore, it holds that for all t‚ąą[0,T]t\in[0,T],

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Ąô~‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąętT‚ąí1‚ąíŌĀ22‚Äč‚ąĎi=1dőłi2‚ÄčVsi‚Äčd‚Äčs)‚ą£‚ĄĪt]=exp‚Ā°((1‚ąíŌĀ2)‚Äč‚ąĎi=1d‚ąętT(‚ąíőłi22+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg~ti‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)\mathbb{E}^{\tilde{\mathbb{P}}}\Big[\exp\Big(\int\_{t}^{T}-\frac{1-\rho^{2}}{2}\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\theta\_{i}^{2}V^{i}\_{s}ds\Big)\mid\mathcal{F}\_{t}\Big]=\exp\Big((1-\rho^{2})\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{t}^{T}\big(-\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)\tilde{g}^{i}\_{t}(s)ds\Big) |  |

Consequently, ([3.59](#S3.E59 "In Proposition 3.9. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) holds and Ōą‚ąąL2‚Äč([0,T],(‚ĄĚd)‚ąó)\psi\in L^{2}([0,T],(\mathbb{R}^{d})^{\*}) solves the inhomogeneous Ricatti-Volterra equation ([3.57](#S3.E57 "In Proposition 3.9. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"))- ([3.58](#S3.E58 "In Proposition 3.9. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")).
Note that for every t‚ąą[0,T]t\in[0,T], Equation ([3.59](#S3.E59 "In Proposition 3.9. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) implies straightforwardly that őďt>0\Gamma\_{t}>0, ‚Ąô‚ąía.s.\mathbb{P}-a.s..
Now, we set

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Gt=‚ąĎi=1d‚ąętT(‚ąíőłi22+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg~ti‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs,t‚Č§T.G\_{t}=\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{t}^{T}\big(-\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)\tilde{g}^{i}\_{t}(s)ds,\quad t\leq T. |  |

Then, őď=exp‚Ā°(G)\Gamma=\exp(G) and d‚Äčőďt=őďt‚Äč(d‚ÄčGt+12‚Äčd‚Äč‚ü®G‚ü©t).d\Gamma\_{t}=\Gamma\_{t}\Big(dG\_{t}+\frac{1}{2}d\langle G\rangle\_{t}\Big).
The dynamics of GG can readily be obtained by recalling g~t‚Äč(s)\tilde{g}\_{t}(s) from ([2.19](#S2.E19 "In 2.2 Formulation of the stochastic Market model ‚Ä£ 2 Preliminaries: Multivariate fake stationary affine Volterra models ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) and by observing that for fixed ss, the dynamics of t‚Üíg~t‚Äč(s)t\to\tilde{g}\_{t}(s) are given by d‚Äčg~t‚Äč(s)=K‚Äč(s‚ąít)‚Äčd‚ÄčZ~tt‚Č§s.d\tilde{g}\_{t}(s)=K(s-t)\,d\tilde{Z}\_{t}\quad t\leq s.
Since g~t‚Äč(t)=Vt\tilde{g}\_{t}(t)=V\_{t}, it follows by stochastic Fubini‚Äôs theorem, see Veraar ([2012](#bib.bib32), Theorem 2.2), that the dynamics of GG reads as

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | d‚ÄčGt\displaystyle dG\_{t} | =(‚ąĎi=1d(őłi22‚ąíFi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚ÄčVti)‚Äčd‚Äčt+‚ąĎi=1d‚ąętTKi‚Äč(s‚ąít)‚Äč(‚ąíőłi22+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčūĚĎĎZ~ti\displaystyle=\;\Big(\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\big(\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}-F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)V^{i}\_{t}\Big)dt+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{t}^{T}{K\_{i}}(s-t)\big(-\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)dsd\tilde{Z}^{i}\_{t} |  |

where we changed variables and used the Riccati‚ÄďVolterra equation ([3.58](#S3.E58 "In Proposition 3.9. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) for Ōą\psi for the last equality. This yields that
the dynamics of őď\Gamma is given by

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | d‚Äčőďt\displaystyle d\Gamma\_{t} | =őďt‚Äč(‚ąĎi=1d(őłi22‚ąíőĹi22‚Äč(1‚ąíŌĀ2)‚Äč(Ōāi‚Äč(t)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąít))2)‚ÄčVti+‚ąĎi=1dőĹi22‚Äč(Ōāi‚Äč(t)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąít))2‚ÄčVti)‚Äčd‚Äčt\displaystyle=\;\Gamma\_{t}\Big(\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\Big(\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}-\frac{\nu\_{i}^{2}}{2}(1-\rho^{2})(\varsigma^{i}(t)\psi^{i}(T-t))^{2}\Big)V^{i}\_{t}+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\frac{\nu\_{i}^{2}}{2}(\varsigma^{i}(t)\psi^{i}(T-t))^{2}V^{i}\_{t}\Big)dt |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | +őďt‚Äč‚ąĎi=1dŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąít)‚ÄčőĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(t)‚ÄčVti‚Äčd‚ÄčW~ti=őďt‚Äč[(12‚Äč|őĽt|2+12‚Äč|ő£‚Äčőõt|2)‚Äčd‚Äčt+őõt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčW~t],\displaystyle\quad\quad+\;\Gamma\_{t}\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\psi^{i}(T-t)\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(t)\sqrt{V^{i}\_{t}}d\widetilde{W}^{i}\_{t}=\;\Gamma\_{t}\Big[\big(\frac{1}{2}\left|\lambda\_{t}\right|^{2}+\frac{1}{2}\left|\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right|^{2}\big)dt+\Lambda\_{t}^{\top}d\widetilde{W}\_{t}\Big], |  |

As 0<őďt‚Č§10<\Gamma\_{t}\leq 1, ‚Ąô‚ąía.s.\mathbb{P}-a.s., we have that őď‚ąąūĚēäūĚĒĹ‚ąě‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚ)\Gamma\in\mathbb{S}^{\infty}\_{\mathbb{F}}([0,T],\mathbb{R}). As for őõ\Lambda, it is clear that it belongs to LūĚĒĹ2‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚd)L^{2}\_{\mathbb{F}}([0,T],\mathbb{R}^{d}) since Ōā\varsigma and Ōą\psi are bounded, Ōą\psi is continuous thus bounded and ūĚĒľ‚Äč[‚ąę0T‚ąĎi=1dVsi‚Äčd‚Äčs]<‚ąě\mathbb{E}\Big[\int\_{0}^{T}\sum\_{i=1}^{d}V^{i}\_{s}ds\Big]<\infty by ([2.17](#S2.E17 "In Theorem 2.7. ‚Ä£ 2.2 Formulation of the stochastic Market model ‚Ä£ 2 Preliminaries: Multivariate fake stationary affine Volterra models ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")). Consequently,
(őď,őõ)‚ąąūĚēäūĚĒĹ‚ąě‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚ)√óLūĚĒĹ2‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚd)\left(\Gamma,\Lambda\right)\in\mathbb{S}^{\infty}\_{\mathbb{F}}([0,T],\mathbb{R})\times L^{2}\_{\mathbb{F}}([0,T],\mathbb{R}^{d}). This complete the Proof ‚Ė°\Box

Proof of Theorem [3.10](#S3.ThmTheorem10 "Theorem 3.10. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") :
We show that JtőĪJ\_{t}^{\alpha} fulfills the martingale optimality principle.
For the first condition, note that őďT=1\Gamma\_{T}=1 and hence JTőĪ=‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚ÄčXTőĪ)J\_{T}^{\alpha}=-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma X^{\alpha}\_{T}\right). Since őď0\Gamma\_{0} is a constant independent of őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in{\mathcal{A}}, J0őĪ=‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚Äčőď0J^{\alpha}\_{0}=-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int\_{0}^{T}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)\Gamma\_{0} is a constant independent of őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in{\mathcal{A}} and thus the second condition is also satisfied.
In order to show that the third condition is also fulfilled, we apply It√ī‚Äôs formula on JtőĪJ\_{t}^{\alpha}.
Setting Yt:=‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčXtőĪ)Y\_{t}:=-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}X^{\alpha}\_{t}\right), we write by It√ī‚Äôs lemma:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | d‚ÄčYt\displaystyle dY\_{t} | =(ő≥‚Äčr‚Äč(s)‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčXtőĪ‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äč(r‚Äč(t)‚ÄčXtőĪ+őĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĽt)+ő≥22‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĪt‚Äče‚ąętT2‚Äčr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)‚ÄčYt‚Äčd‚Äčt‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčYt‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčBt\displaystyle=\left(\gamma r(s)e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}X^{\alpha}\_{t}-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\big(r(t)X^{\alpha}\_{t}+\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\lambda\_{t}\big)+\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\alpha\_{t}e^{\int\_{t}^{T}2r(s)ds}\right)Y\_{t}dt-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}Y\_{t}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}dB\_{t} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĽt+ő≥22‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĪt‚Äče‚ąętT2‚Äčr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)‚ÄčYt‚Äčd‚Äčt‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčYt‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčBt\displaystyle=\left(-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\lambda\_{t}+\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\alpha\_{t}e^{\int\_{t}^{T}2r(s)ds}\right)Y\_{t}dt-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}Y\_{t}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}dB\_{t} |  |

Consequently, by It√ī‚Äôs product rule, one may write

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | d‚ÄčJtőĪ=\displaystyle dJ\_{t}^{\alpha}= | Yt‚Äčőďt‚Äč[(12‚Äč|őĽt|2+12‚Äč|ő£‚Äčőõt|2)‚Äčd‚Äčt+őõt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčW~t]+Yt‚Äčőďt‚Äč(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĽt+ő≥22‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĪt‚Äče‚ąętT2‚Äčr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)‚Äčd‚Äčt\displaystyle\;Y\_{t}\Gamma\_{t}\Big[\big(\frac{1}{2}\left|\lambda\_{t}\right|^{2}+\frac{1}{2}\left|\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right|^{2}\big)dt+\Lambda\_{t}^{\top}d\widetilde{W}\_{t}\Big]+Y\_{t}\Gamma\_{t}\left(-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\lambda\_{t}+\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\alpha\_{t}e^{\int\_{t}^{T}2r(s)ds}\right)dt |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | ‚ąíYt‚Äčőďt‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčBt‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äč(ő£‚Äčőõt)‚ÄčYt‚Äčőďt‚Äčd‚Äčt\displaystyle-Y\_{t}\Gamma\_{t}\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}dB\_{t}-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\alpha^{\top}\_{t}\left(\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right)Y\_{t}\Gamma\_{t}dt |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =JtőĪ‚Äč(ő≥22‚Äče‚ąętT2‚Äčr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĪt‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚ÄčőĽt‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äč(ő£‚Äčőõt)+12‚Äč(|őĽt|2+|ő£‚Äčőõt|2)+őõt‚ä§‚Äčő£‚ÄčőĽt)‚Äčd‚Äčt\displaystyle=\;J\_{t}^{\alpha}\Big(\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}e^{\int\_{t}^{T}2r(s)ds}\alpha^{\top}\_{t}\alpha\_{t}-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}\lambda\_{t}-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\alpha^{\top}\_{t}\left(\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right)+\frac{1}{2}(\left|\lambda\_{t}\right|^{2}+\left|\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right|^{2})+\Lambda\_{t}^{\top}\Sigma\lambda\_{t}\Big)dt |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | ‚ąíő≥‚ÄčJtőĪ‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčBt+JtőĪ‚Äčőõt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčWt=JtőĪ‚ÄčDt‚Äč(őĪt)‚Äčd‚Äčt‚ąíő≥‚ÄčJtőĪ‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčBt+JtőĪ‚Äčőõt‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčWt.\displaystyle-\gamma J\_{t}^{\alpha}e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}dB\_{t}+J\_{t}^{\alpha}\Lambda\_{t}^{\top}dW\_{t}=J\_{t}^{\alpha}D\_{t}(\alpha\_{t})dt-\gamma J\_{t}^{\alpha}e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\alpha\_{t}^{\top}dB\_{t}+J\_{t}^{\alpha}\Lambda\_{t}^{\top}dW\_{t}. |  |

where the drift factor takes the form:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Dt‚Äč(őĪ)=\displaystyle D\_{t}(\alpha)= | ő≥22‚Äče‚ąętT2‚Äčr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪ‚ä§‚ÄčőĪ‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčőĪ‚ä§‚Äč(őĽt+ő£‚Äčőõt)+12‚Äč|őĽt+ő£‚Äčőõt|2.\displaystyle\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}e^{\int\_{t}^{T}2r(s)ds}\alpha^{\top}\alpha-\gamma e^{\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\alpha^{\top}\big(\lambda\_{t}+\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\big)+\frac{1}{2}\left|\lambda\_{t}+\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right|^{2}. |  |

Differentiating Dt‚Äč(őĪ)D\_{t}(\alpha) with respect to őĪ\alpha and checking the second order condition, the maximizer őĪt‚ąó=1ő≥‚Äče‚ąí‚ąętTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äč(őĽt+ő£‚Äčőõt)\alpha^{\*}\_{t}=\frac{1}{\gamma}e^{-\int\_{t}^{T}r(s)ds}\left(\lambda\_{t}+\Sigma\Lambda\_{t}\right) for every t‚ąą[0,T]t\in[0,T] that is the strategy given by Equation ([3.64](#S3.E64 "In Theorem 3.10. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")).
Evaluating the drift factor DtD\_{t} at őĪt‚ąó\alpha^{\*}\_{t} show that Dt‚Äč(őĪt‚ąó)D\_{t}(\alpha^{\*}\_{t}) vanishes to 0. Note Dt‚Äč(őĪ)D\_{t}(\alpha) is a quadratic function on őĪ\alpha and ő≥‚ąí1<0\gamma-1<0. As Dt‚Äč(őĪt‚ąó)=0D\_{t}(\alpha^{\*}\_{t})=0, then Dt‚Äč(őĪt)‚Č•0D\_{t}(\alpha\_{t})\geq 0 for any admissible strategy őĪ\alpha.
Moreover, solving the stochastic differential equation for JtőĪJ\_{t}^{\alpha} yields

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ‚ąÄt‚ąą[0,T],JtőĪ=‚ąíőď0ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚Äče‚ąę0tDs‚Äč(őĪs)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ÄčFtőĪ\displaystyle\hskip 85.35826pt\forall\,t\in[0,T],\quad J\_{t}^{\alpha}=-\frac{\Gamma\_{0}}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int\_{0}^{T}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)e^{\int^{t}\_{0}D\_{s}(\alpha\_{s})ds}F\_{t}^{\alpha} |  |
|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | whereFtőĪ=‚Ąį‚Äč(‚ąę0t‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪs‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčBs+őõs‚ä§‚Äčd‚ÄčWs)\displaystyle\text{where}\quad F\_{t}^{\alpha}=\mathcal{E}\Big(\int\_{0}^{t}-\gamma e^{\int\_{s}^{T}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\top}dB\_{s}+\Lambda\_{s}^{\top}dW\_{s}\Big) |  |
|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | =exp‚Ā°(‚ąí12‚Äč‚ąę0t(ő≥2‚Äče2‚Äč‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs|2+|őõs|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ąíő≥‚Äč‚ąę0te‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪs‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs+‚ąę0tőõs‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎWs).\displaystyle\hskip 56.9055pt=\operatorname{exp}\Big(-\frac{1}{2}\int^{t}\_{0}\Big(\gamma^{2}e^{2\int\_{s}^{T}r(u)du}\left|\alpha\_{s}\right|^{2}+\left|\Lambda\_{s}\right|^{2}\Big)ds-\gamma\int\_{0}^{t}e^{\int\_{s}^{T}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\top}dB\_{s}+\int\_{0}^{t}\Lambda\_{s}^{\top}dW\_{s}\Big). |  |

Note Dt‚Äč(őĪt‚ąó)=0D\_{t}(\alpha^{\*}\_{t})=0, then Dt‚Äč(őĪt)‚Č•0D\_{t}(\alpha\_{t})\geq 0.
By our assumptions on the admissible strategies [3.8](#S3.ThmTheorem8 "Definition 3.8. ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") and Proposition [3.9](#S3.ThmTheorem9 "Proposition 3.9. ‚Ä£ 3.2.1 The degenerate correlation case ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"),
(őĪ,őõ)‚ąąLūĚĒĹ2,l‚Äčo‚Äčc‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚd)\left(\alpha,\Lambda\right)\in{L^{2,loc}\_{\mathbb{F}}([0,T],\mathbb{R}^{d})} and thus, the stochastic exponential FtőĪF\_{t}^{\alpha} is a local martingale (which follows from the basic properties of the Dool√©ans-Dade exponential). Therefore, there exists a sequence of stopping times {ŌĄn}n‚Č•1\{\tau\_{n}\}\_{n\geq 1} satisfying limn‚Üí‚ąěŌĄn=T\lim\_{n\rightarrow\infty}\tau\_{n}=T, ‚Ąô\mathbb{P}-a.s., such that that Ft‚ąßŌĄnőĪF^{\alpha}\_{t\wedge\tau\_{n}} is a positive martingale for every nn.

Furthermore, ‚ąíőď0ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°[‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äčx0]‚Äče‚ąę0tDs‚Äč(őĪs)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs-\frac{\Gamma\_{0}}{\gamma}\exp\big[-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(u)du}x\_{0}\big]e^{\int^{t}\_{0}D\_{s}(\alpha\_{s})ds} is non-increasing. Therefore, Jt‚ąßŌĄnőĪJ^{\alpha}\_{t\wedge\tau\_{n}} is a supermartingale. Then for s‚Č§ts\leq t, ūĚĒľ‚Äč[Jt‚ąßŌĄnőĪ|‚ĄĪs]‚Č§Js‚ąßŌĄnőĪ\mathbb{E}[J^{\alpha}\_{t\wedge\tau\_{n}}|{\mathcal{F}}\_{s}]\leq J^{\alpha}\_{s\wedge\tau\_{n}}. It implies that for any set A‚ąą‚ĄĪsA\in{\mathcal{F}}\_{s},

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[Jt‚ąßŌĄnőĪ‚ÄčūĚüôA]‚Č§ūĚĒľ‚Äč[Js‚ąßŌĄnőĪ‚ÄčūĚüôA],s‚Č§t.\mathbb{E}[J^{\alpha}\_{t\wedge\tau\_{n}}\mathds{1}\_{A}]\leq\mathbb{E}[J^{\alpha}\_{s\wedge\tau\_{n}}\mathds{1}\_{A}],\quad s\leq t. |  |

for every nn. Since (exp‚Ā°[‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąęt‚ąßŌĄnTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčXt‚ąßŌĄn])n\left(\exp\big[-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{t\wedge\tau\_{n}}r(u)du}X\_{t\wedge\tau\_{n}}\big]\right)\_{n} is uniformly integrable (Definition [3.8](#S3.ThmTheorem8 "Definition 3.8. ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) and őď\Gamma is bounded, (Jt‚ąßŌĄnőĪ)n\left(J^{\alpha}\_{t\wedge\tau\_{n}}\right)\_{n} and (Js‚ąßŌĄnőĪ)n\left(J^{\alpha}\_{s\wedge\tau\_{n}}\right)\_{n} are uniformly integrable. Let n‚Üí‚ąěn\rightarrow\infty, then ūĚĒľ‚Äč[JtőĪ‚ÄčūĚüôA]‚Č§ūĚĒľ‚Äč[JsőĪ‚ÄčūĚüôA]\mathbb{E}[J^{\alpha}\_{t}\mathds{1}\_{A}]\leq\mathbb{E}[J^{\alpha}\_{s}\mathds{1}\_{A}]. Then we deduce that JőĪJ^{\alpha} is a supermartingale for every arbitrary admissible strategy őĪ\alpha.
  
It remains to show that JtőĪ‚ąóJ\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}} is a true martingale for the optimal strategy őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*} in which case e‚ąę0tDs‚Äč(őĪs‚ąó)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs=1e^{\int\_{0}^{t}D\_{s}(\alpha\_{s}^{\*})ds}=1 and hence JtőĪ‚ąó=‚ąíőď0ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚ÄčFtőĪ‚ąóJ\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}}=-\frac{\Gamma\_{0}}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int\_{0}^{T}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)F\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}}.

For őĪt=őĪt‚ąó\alpha\_{t}=\alpha^{\*}\_{t}, FtőĪ‚ąóF\_{t}^{\alpha^{\*}} is a martingale by Lemma [5.1](#S5.ThmTheorem1 "Lemma 5.1 (Martingale property of stochastic exponentials). ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") with g1,i‚Äč(t)=‚ąíŌĀi‚Äčőłi+(1‚ąíŌĀi2)‚ÄčőĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(t)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąít)‚ąąL‚ąě‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚ)g\_{1,i}(t)=-\rho\_{i}\theta\_{i}+(1-\rho\_{i}^{2})\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(t)\psi^{i}(T-t)\in L^{\infty}([0,T],\mathbb{R}) and g2,i‚Äč(t)=‚ąí1‚ąíŌĀi2‚Äč(őłi+ŌĀi‚ÄčőĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(t)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąít))‚ąąL‚ąě‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚ)g\_{2,i}(t)=-\sqrt{1-\rho\_{i}^{2}}\big(\theta\_{i}+\rho\_{i}\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(t)\psi^{i}(T-t)\big)\in L^{\infty}([0,T],\mathbb{R}) for 1‚Č§i‚Č§d1\leq i\leq d.
Subsequently, JtőĪ‚ąóJ^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{t} is a true martingale. We have verified all conditions required by martingale optimality principle in Definition [3.2](#S3.ThmTheorem2 "Definition 3.2 (Martingale optimality principle). ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"), except for the admissibility of őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*}, which follows directly from Step 1 in the proof of Theorem [3.12](#S3.ThmTheorem12 "Theorem 3.12. ‚Ä£ 3.2.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") below in the more general setting, as the arguments are similar. The proof is complete. ‚Ė°\Box

Proof of Theorem [3.12](#S3.ThmTheorem12 "Theorem 3.12. ‚Ä£ 3.2.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"):

Step 1 (Proof of Admissibility:)
We begin by proving the admissibility of the candidate in equation ([3.77](#S3.E77 "In 3.2.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) for the optimal portfolio strategy őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*}, and, on the way,
we deduce the bound in equation ([3.80](#S3.E80 "In Theorem 3.12. ‚Ä£ 3.2.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")).

In order to show that őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*} is admissible, we have to show that (a), (b), (c) of Definition [3.8](#S3.ThmTheorem8 "Definition 3.8. ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") hold. Part (b) is true because ([3.53](#S3.E53 "In 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) has a unique solution ([3.54](#S3.E54 "In 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) in terms of (S,V,B)(S,V,B).
To prove (c), that is {exp‚Ā°[‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąęŌĄTrv‚ÄčūĚĎĎv‚ÄčXŌĄőĪ‚ąó]:ŌĄ‚Äč¬†stopping time with values in¬†‚Äč[0,T]}\left\{\exp\big[-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{\tau}r\_{v}dv}X^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{\tau}\big]:\tau\text{ stopping time with values in }[0,T]\right\} is a uniformly integrable family, we only need to show

| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | supŌĄūĚĒľ‚Äč[e‚ąíp‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąęŌĄTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčXŌĄőĪ‚ąó]<‚ąě,¬†for some¬†‚Äčp>1.\sup\_{\tau}\mathbb{E}\Big[e^{-p\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{\tau}r(u)du}X^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{\tau}}\Big]<\infty,\text{ for some }p>1. |  | (5.100) |

then:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[e‚ąíp‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąęŌĄTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčXŌĄőĪ‚ąó]\displaystyle\mathbb{E}\Big[e^{-p\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{\tau}r(u)du}X^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{\tau}}\Big] | ‚Č§e‚ąíp‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äčx0‚ÄčūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąíp‚Äčő≥‚Äč‚ąę0ŌĄe‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčőĽs‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚ąíp‚Äčő≥‚Äč‚ąę0ŌĄe‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs)]\displaystyle\leq e^{-p\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(u)du}x\_{0}}\mathbb{E}\Big[\exp\Big(-p\gamma\int^{\tau}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\lambda\_{s}ds-p\gamma\int^{\tau}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}dB\_{s}\Big)\Big] |  |

|  |  | ‚Č§e‚ąíp‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äčx0ūĚĒľ[exp(pő≥‚ąę0Te‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu|őĪs‚ąó‚ä§őĽs|ds+p2ő≥2‚ąę0Te‚ąęsT2‚Äčr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu|őĪs‚ąó|2ds)\displaystyle\leq e^{-p\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(u)du}x\_{0}}\mathbb{E}\Big[\exp\Big(p\gamma\int^{T}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\big|\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\lambda\_{s}\big|ds+p^{2}\gamma^{2}\int^{T}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}2r(u)du}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}ds\Big) |  |

so that by H√∂lder‚Äôs inequality, followed by the elementary inequality a‚Äčb‚Č§(a2+b2)/2ab\leq(a^{2}+b^{2})/2 in the third line, we may write

|  |  |  |

|  | supŌĄūĚĒľ‚Äč[e‚ąíp‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąęŌĄTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčXŌĄőĪ‚ąó]‚Č§e‚ąíp‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äčx0‚ÄčūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąę0T(2‚Äčp2‚Äčő≥2‚Äče‚ąęsT2‚Äčr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó|2+2‚Äčp‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčőĽs|)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)]12\displaystyle\,\sup\_{\tau}\mathbb{E}\Big[e^{-p\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{\tau}r(u)du}X^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{\tau}}\Big]\leq e^{-p\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(u)du}x\_{0}}\mathbb{E}\Big[\exp\Big(\int^{T}\_{0}(2p^{2}\gamma^{2}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}2r(u)du}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}+2p\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\big|\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\lambda\_{s}\big|)ds\Big)\Big]^{\frac{1}{2}} |  |
|  |  |  |

|  | √ósupŌĄūĚĒľ[exp(‚ąí2p2ő≥2‚ąę0ŌĄe‚ąęsT2‚Äčr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu|őĪs‚ąó|2ds‚ąí2pő≥‚ąę0ŌĄe‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎuőĪs‚ąó‚ä§dBs)]12\displaystyle\hskip 128.0374pt\times\sup\_{\tau}\mathbb{E}\Big[\exp\Big(-2p^{2}\gamma^{2}\int^{\tau}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}2r(u)du}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}ds-2p\gamma\int^{\tau}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}dB\_{s}\Big)\Big]^{\frac{1}{2}} |  |
|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ‚Č§e‚ąíp‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äčx02‚Äč(ūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(4‚Äčp2‚Äčő≥2‚Äč‚ąę0Te‚ąęsT2‚Äčr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)]+ūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(4‚Äčp‚Äčő≥‚Äč‚ąę0Te‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčőĽs|‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)])12√ó1\displaystyle\;\leq\frac{e^{-p\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(u)du}x\_{0}}}{\sqrt{2}}\Big(\mathbb{E}\big[\exp\big(4p^{2}\gamma^{2}\int^{T}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}2r(u)du}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}ds\big)\big]+\mathbb{E}\big[\exp\big(4p\gamma\int^{T}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\big|\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\lambda\_{s}\big|ds\big)\big]\Big)^{\frac{1}{2}}\times 1 |  |

which is finite since on the first hand, the Dol√©ans-Dade exponential ‚Ąį‚Äč(‚ąí‚ąę0‚čÖ2‚Äčp‚Äčő≥‚Äče‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs)\mathcal{E}\big(-\int\_{0}^{\cdot}2p\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}dB\_{s}\big) satisfies the Novikov‚Äôs condition by virtue of ([3.27](#S3.E27 "In 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")), and is therefore a true martingale (see also Lemma [5.2](#S5.ThmTheorem2 "Lemma 5.2 (Martingale property). ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) with Expectation 11. Then by optional sampling theorem with the fact that ŌĄ‚Č§T\tau\leq T, it follows that the supremum is bounded by 11.

On the others hand, we used Jensen‚Äôs inequality to obtain the bound

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | e2‚Äč‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó|2=1ő≥2‚Äč|őĽs+ő£‚Äčőõs|2‚Č§2ő≥2‚Äč(|őĽs|2+|ő£‚Äčőõs|2)‚Č§2ő≥2‚Äč(1+|ő£|2)‚Äč(|őĽs|2+|őõs|2)e^{2\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}=\frac{1}{\gamma^{2}}|\lambda\_{s}+\Sigma\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}\leq\frac{2}{\gamma^{2}}(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Sigma\Lambda\_{s}|^{2})\leq\frac{2}{\gamma^{2}}(1+|\Sigma|^{2})(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}) |  |

so that the first term in the bracket is finite thanks to condition ([3.27](#S3.E27 "In 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) with constant a‚Äč(p)=2‚Äč(8‚Äčp2‚ąí2‚Äčp)‚Äč(1+|ő£|2)a(p)=2(8p^{2}{-2p})\left(1+|{\Sigma}|^{2}\right) after noticing that 8‚Äčp2‚Č§2‚Äč(8‚Äčp2‚ąí2‚Äčp)8p^{2}\leq 2(8p^{2}{-2p}) for all p>1p>1.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(4‚Äčp2‚Äčő≥2‚Äč‚ąę0Te‚ąęsT2‚Äčr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)]‚Č§ūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(a‚Äč(p)‚Äč‚ąę0T(|őĽs|2+|őõs|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)]<‚ąě,\mathbb{E}\Big[\exp\big(4p^{2}\gamma^{2}\int^{T}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}2r(u)du}\left|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}\right|^{2}ds\big)\Big]\leq\mathbb{E}\left[\exp\left({a(p)\int\_{0}^{T}\left(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}\right)ds}\right)\right]<\infty, |  | (5.101) |

Still owing to the elementary inequality |a‚Äčb|‚Č§(|a|2+|b|2)/2|ab|\leq(|a|^{2}+|b|^{2})/2, we have

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | e‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčőĽs|=1ő≥‚Äč(|őĽs|2+|(ő£‚Äčőõs)‚ä§‚ÄčőĽs|)‚Č§1ő≥‚Äč(|őĽs|2+|ő£|‚Äč|őĽs|2+|őõs|22)‚Č§12‚Äčő≥‚Äč(2+|ő£|)‚Äč(|őĽs|2+|őõs|2)e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}|\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\lambda\_{s}|=\frac{1}{\gamma}\big(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|(\Sigma\Lambda\_{s})^{\top}\lambda\_{s}|\big)\leq\frac{1}{\gamma}(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Sigma|\frac{|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}}{2})\leq\frac{1}{2\gamma}(2+|\Sigma|)(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}) |  |

which ensures that the second term in the bracket is finite i.e.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(4‚Äčp‚Äčő≥‚Äč‚ąę0Te‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs‚ąó‚ä§‚ÄčőĽs|‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)]‚Č§ūĚĒľ‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(a‚Äč(2‚Äčp)‚Äč‚ąę0T(|őĽs|2+|őõs|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)]<‚ąě,\mathbb{E}\Big[\exp\big(4p\gamma\int^{T}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\big|\alpha\_{s}^{\*\top}\lambda\_{s}\big|ds\big)\Big]\leq\mathbb{E}\left[\exp\left({a(2p)\int\_{0}^{T}\left(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}\right)ds}\right)\right]<\infty, |  | (5.102) |

thanks to condition ([3.27](#S3.E27 "In 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) with constant a‚Äč(2‚Äčp)=2‚Äčp‚Äč(2+|ő£|)a(2p)=2p\left(2+|{\Sigma}|\right).
We are left to prove that őĪ‚ąó‚ąąLūĚĒĹ2‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚd)\alpha^{\*}\in L^{2}\_{\mathbb{F}}([0,T],\mathbb{R}^{d}). We have:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľ‚Äč[‚ąę0T|őĪs‚ąó|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs]\displaystyle\mathbb{E}\left[\int\_{0}^{T}|\alpha\_{s}^{\*}|^{2}ds\right] | =ūĚĒľ‚Äč[‚ąę0T1ő≥2‚Äče‚ąí2‚Äč‚ąęsTr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äč|őĽs+ő£‚Äčőõs|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs]‚Č§ūĚĒľ‚Äč[2ő≥2‚Äč(1+|ő£|2)‚Äč‚ąę0T(|őĽs|2+|őõs|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs]<‚ąě,\displaystyle{=}\mathbb{E}\left[\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{1}{\gamma^{2}}e^{-2\int\_{s}^{T}r(s)ds}|\lambda\_{s}+\Sigma\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}ds\right]\leq\mathbb{E}\left[\frac{2}{\gamma^{2}}(1+|\Sigma|^{2})\int\_{0}^{T}\left(|\lambda\_{s}|^{2}+|\Lambda\_{s}|^{2}\right)ds\right]<\infty, |  |

where the last term is finite due to condition ([3.27](#S3.E27 "In 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) and the inequality |z|q‚Č§cq‚Äče|z|,‚ąÄq‚Č•1|z|^{q}\leq c\_{q}e^{|z|},\;\forall\,q\geq 1.
It becomes straightforward that őĪ‚ąó\alpha^{\*} in equation ([3.77](#S3.E77 "In 3.2.2 The general correlation case: A verification argument ‚Ä£ 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) is admissible.

Step 2 (Proof of the equality (1):)
Let‚Äôs us consider the Problem ([3.56](#S3.E56 "In 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) with an arbitrary strategy őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in\mathcal{A}.

where the last inequality comes from the fact that FTőĪ‚ąóF\_{T}^{\alpha^{\*}} is a true martingale. This completes the first part (1)(1) of the proof.
It remains to show the inequality (2) for arbitrary admissible portfolio strategies őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in\mathcal{A}.

Step 3 (Proof of the inequality (2):)
Note that the SDE for the wealth process ([3.54](#S3.E54 "In 3.2 Optimal strategy for the exponential utility maximization problem ‚Ä£ 3 Merton‚Äôs portfolio problem: Utility maximisation ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) can be solved explicitly so as to admit the representation

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | XTőĪ=e‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0+‚ąę0Te‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪs‚ä§‚ÄčőĽs‚Äčds+‚ąę0Te‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪs‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs.X\_{T}^{\alpha}=e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(s)ds}x\_{0}+\int^{T}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\top}\lambda\_{s}\mathrm{d}s+\int^{T}\_{0}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\top}dB\_{s}. |  | (5.104) |

Since őĪt\alpha\_{t} is bounded by assumption and s‚Üíe‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ąąL‚ąě‚Äč([0,T],‚ĄĚ)s\to e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\in L^{\infty}([0,T],\mathbb{R}), we can define a new probability measure ‚Ąö\mathbb{Q} with Radon-Nikodym density

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ZT:=d‚Äč‚Ąöd‚Äč‚Ąô|‚ĄĪT=exp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äč‚ąę0Te‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪs‚ä§‚ÄčūĚĎĎBs‚ąíő≥22‚Äč‚ąę0Te2‚Äč‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs|2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs),{Z}\_{T}:=\frac{d{\mathbb{Q}}}{d\mathbb{P}}|\_{\mathcal{F}\_{T}}=\exp\Big(-\gamma\int\_{0}^{T}e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\top}\,dB\_{s}-\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}\int\_{0}^{T}e^{2\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\left|\alpha\_{s}\right|^{2}ds\Big), |  | (5.105) |

by Lemma [5.2](#S5.ThmTheorem2 "Lemma 5.2 (Martingale property). ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"). |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľx0,V0‚Äč[U‚Äč(XTőĪ)]\displaystyle\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}\Big[U(X\_{T}^{\alpha})\Big] | =‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚ÄčūĚĒľx0,V0‚Ąö‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąę0T(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪs‚ä§‚ÄčőĽs+ő≥22‚Äče2‚Äč‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚Äč|őĪs|2)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)],\displaystyle\,=-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}^{\mathbb{Q}}\Big[\exp\Big(\int\_{0}^{T}\big(-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\alpha\_{s}^{\top}\lambda\_{s}+\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}e^{2\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\left|\alpha\_{s}\right|^{2}\big)ds\Big)\Big], |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚ÄčūĚĒľx0,V0‚Ąö‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąę0TFsőĪ‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)],\displaystyle=-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}^{\mathbb{Q}}\Big[\exp\Big(\int\_{0}^{T}F\_{s}^{\alpha}ds\Big)\Big], |  |

with the real-valued deterministic process FsF\_{s} given by

|  |  |  |  |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | =‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0T(‚ąíőłi22+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg0i‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)\displaystyle\hskip 128.0374pt=-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)\exp\Big(\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\big(-\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)g^{i}\_{0}(s)ds\Big) |  |
|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | √óūĚĒľx0,V0‚Ąö[exp(‚ąí‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0TőĹi22(Ōāi(s)Ōąi(T‚ąís))2Vsids+‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0TőĹiŌāi(s)Ōąi(T‚ąís)VsidW^si\displaystyle\hskip 79.6678pt\times\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}^{\mathbb{Q}}\Big[\exp\Big(-\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{\nu\_{i}^{2}}{2}(\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s))^{2}V\_{s}^{i}ds+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s)\sqrt{V\_{s}^{i}}d\widehat{W}^{i}\_{s} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | +‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0Tő≥22e2‚Äč‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎuŌÄ^s,i2Vsids)].\displaystyle\hskip 170.71652pt+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}e^{2\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\hat{\pi}\_{s,i}^{2}V^{i}\_{s}\,ds\Big)\Big]. |  | (5.107) |

Remark: (Alternative Proof of the equality (1):) At this stage, note that if the admissible strategy őĪ\alpha is optimal, i.e. őĪ=őĪ‚ąó\alpha=\alpha^{\*} so that ŌÄ^‚Č°0\hat{\pi}\equiv 0 and ‚Ąö‚Č°‚Ąö‚ąó\mathbb{Q}\equiv\mathbb{Q}^{\*} in ([5.105](#S5.E105 "In 5.2 Proofs of Proposition 3.9 and Theorems 3.10 and 3.12 ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")), then Equation ([5.107](#S5.E107 "In 5.2 Proofs of Proposition 3.9 and Theorems 3.10 and 3.12 ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")) becomes:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | ūĚĒľx0,V0‚Äč[‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚ÄčXTőĪ‚ąó)]=‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0T(‚ąíőłi22+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg0i‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)\displaystyle\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}\Big[-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma X^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{T}\right)\Big]=-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)\exp\Big(\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\big(-\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)g^{i}\_{0}(s)ds\Big) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | √óūĚĒľx0,V0‚Ąö‚ąó‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąí‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0TőĹi22‚Äč(Ōāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąís))2‚ÄčVsi‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0TőĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąís)‚ÄčVsi‚ÄčūĚĎĎW^s‚ąói)].\displaystyle\hskip 62.59596pt\times\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}^{\mathbb{Q}^{\*}}\Big[\exp\Big(-\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{\nu\_{i}^{2}}{2}(\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s))^{2}V\_{s}^{i}ds+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s)\sqrt{V\_{s}^{i}}d\widehat{W}^{\*i}\_{s}\Big)\Big]. |  |

Since Ōą\psi is continuous, it is bounded and therefore the stochastic exponential is a true ‚Ąö‚ąó\mathbb{Q}^{\*}- martingale with expectation 11 by Lemma [5.1](#S5.ThmTheorem1 "Lemma 5.1 (Martingale property of stochastic exponentials). ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models") with g2=0g\_{2}=0 and g1,i‚Äč(s)=őĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąís)g\_{1,i}(s)=\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s) . Thus we get

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľx0,V0‚Äč[‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚ÄčXTőĪ‚ąó)]=‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0T(‚ąíőłi22+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg0i‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs).\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}\Big[-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma X^{\alpha^{\*}}\_{T}\right)\Big]=-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)\exp\Big(\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\big(-\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)g^{i}\_{0}(s)ds\Big). |  |

This completes the first part of the proof (equality (1)).

Back to the proof of the inequality (2) for arbitrary admissible portfolio strategies őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in\mathcal{A}, still from Equation ([5.107](#S5.E107 "In 5.2 Proofs of Proposition 3.9 and Theorems 3.10 and 3.12 ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models")), since VsV\_{s} is positive
definite, the term ‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0Tő≥22‚Äče2‚Äč‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčŌÄ^s,i2‚ÄčVsi‚ÄčūĚĎĎs\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}e^{2\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\hat{\pi}\_{s,i}^{2}V^{i}\_{s}\,ds or equivalently ‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0Tő≥22‚Äče2‚Äč‚ąęsTr‚Äč(u)‚ÄčūĚĎĎu‚ÄčőĪ^s,i2‚ÄčūĚĎĎs\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{\gamma^{2}}{2}e^{2\int^{T}\_{s}r(u)du}\hat{\alpha}\_{s,i}^{2}\,ds has to be more than or equal to 0 so that

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | ūĚĒľx0,V0‚Äč[‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚ÄčXTőĪ)]‚Č§‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0T(‚ąíőłi22+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg0i‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs)\displaystyle\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}\Big[-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma X^{\alpha}\_{T}\right)\Big]\leq-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)\exp\Big(\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\big(-\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)g^{i}\_{0}(s)ds\Big) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | √óūĚĒľx0,V0‚Ąö‚Äč[exp‚Ā°(‚ąí‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0TőĹi22‚Äč(Ōāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąís))2‚ÄčVsi‚ÄčūĚĎĎs+‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0TőĹi‚ÄčŌāi‚Äč(s)‚ÄčŌąi‚Äč(T‚ąís)‚ÄčVsi‚ÄčūĚĎĎW^si)].\displaystyle\hskip 62.59596pt\times\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}^{\mathbb{Q}}\Big[\exp\Big(-\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\frac{\nu\_{i}^{2}}{2}(\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s))^{2}V\_{s}^{i}ds+\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\nu\_{i}\varsigma^{i}(s)\psi^{i}(T-s)\sqrt{V\_{s}^{i}}d\widehat{W}^{i}\_{s}\Big)\Big]. |  |

Since the stochastic exponential
is a ‚Ąö\mathbb{Q}-martingale with expectation 11 still by Lemma [5.1](#S5.ThmTheorem1 "Lemma 5.1 (Martingale property of stochastic exponentials). ‚Ä£ 5 Proofs of the main results ‚Ä£ On Utility Maximization under Multivariate Fake Stationary Affine Volterra Models"), we finally obtain that for every őĪ‚ąąūĚíú\alpha\in\mathcal{A}

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ūĚĒľx0,V0‚Äč[‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚ÄčXTőĪ)]‚Č§‚ąí1ő≥‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąíő≥‚Äče‚ąę0Tr‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs‚Äčx0)‚Äčexp‚Ā°(‚ąĎi=1d‚ąę0T(‚ąíőłi22+Fi‚Äč(s,Ōą‚Äč(T‚ąís)))‚Äčg0i‚Äč(s)‚ÄčūĚĎĎs).\mathbb{E}\_{x\_{0},V\_{0}}{\big[-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma X^{\alpha}\_{T}\right)\big]}\leq-\frac{1}{\gamma}\exp\left(-\gamma e^{\int^{T}\_{0}r(s)ds}x\_{0}\right)\exp\Big(\sum\_{i=1}^{d}\int\_{0}^{T}\big(-\frac{\theta\_{i}^{2}}{2}+F\_{i}(s,\psi(T-s))\big)g^{i}\_{0}(s)ds\Big). |  |

which completes the proof and we are done. ‚Ė°\Box
